langoKamo--human-language sensorial-concept-Mcs
(lagKmo)

McsHitp-creation: {2019-08-30}

overview of lagKmo

description::
· langoKamo is a-constructed oral and alphabetic human-language for the-computer-era that could-be-used as a-common-language.
· langoKamo will-be the-product of an-EVOLUTIONARY process and not a-revolutionary as Esperanto.
· I am-showing the-way.
· the-language must-be-tested and then to be-used.
· also it must-be-open to changes.

semasio-attribute::
1. MOOD: realis, realisNo, imperative, subjunctive.
2. TEMPO: past, present, future.
3. INSTANTNESS: instant, instanctNo-(interval).
4. DIRECTION: active, activeNo-(passive).
5. PERFECTIVENESS: perfective, perfectiveNo-(imperfective).
6. INTERROGATION: interrogative, interrogativeNo.
7. AFFIRMATION: affirmative, affirmativeNo-(negative).
8. NUMBER: singular, plural.
9. PERSON: first, second, third.
· the-number of individual-realis-semasio-verbs is: 1x3x2x2x2x2x2x2x3 = 576.

* lagHmn-semasio-verb,

phonemeKmo.vowelNo of speech

description::
· the-attributes of the-consonant-phonemes must-have, like the-vowels, the-most OPPOSITE characteristics that most different native-speakers of other languages distinguish.
· Greek people for example does-not-distinguish the-diference of h|ĥ and s|ŝ of Εsperanto.

  bilabial labiodent dental alveolar post-
alveolar 		palatal velar
plosive voiceNo /p/ \p\   /t/ \t\ /c/ \kk\ /k/ \k\
voiced /b/ \b\   /d/ \d\ /ɟ/ \gg\ /g/ \g\
fricative voiceNo   /f/ \f\ /θ/ \θ\ /s/ \s\ /ʃ/ \c\ /ç/ \hh\ /x/ \h\
voiced   /v/ \v\ /ð/ \δ\ /z/ \z\ /ʒ/ \j\ /ʝ/ \yy\ /ɣ/ \y\
nasal /m/ \m\   /n/ \n\ /ɲ/ \nn\  
trill       /r/ \r\      
lateral       /l/ \l\   /ʎ/ \ll\

unitLigKmo.letter of text

description::
· letter of langoKamo is the-term-unit of alphabetic-langoKamo.
· in our computer-era, the-keyboards must-contain the-letters.
· I am-using 25 letters that correspond one-to-one to langoKamo's-phonemes (except palatized).
· in the-future a-new alphabet, simpler and denoting the-attributes of the-letters can-be-constructed.
· for example, a-suggesting alphabet is:

· the-above alphabet, denotes the-voiceless ("look" right) and the-voiced ("look" left) phonemes and there-is-no difference between capital[a] and small letters.
· if one knows the-first[a], knows and the-other letter.
· many people can-work on the-new alphabet.
· then we can-choose the-best.

name::
* Mcs.langoKamo-letter!⇒letterKmo,
* Mcs.lagKmo'letter!⇒letterKmo,
* Mcs.lagKmoAbc-letter!⇒letterKmo,

letterKmo.SPECIFIC

specific::
· langoKamo has 25 letters.
· 5 vowels and 20 consonants.
·
· the-order is-based on the-IPA-chart and my goal to use it for the-creation of langoKamo-numerals.

strrUntLigKmo.affix

description::
· affix of langoKamo is its human-affix.
· langoKamo relies heavily on affixes.
· its most important rule is that it uses the-suffixes -o, -i, -a to denote its semasio-concepts sms-noun, sms-verb, sms-conjunction respectively.
· BUT, because anyone can-make mistakes using its affix-rules, and will-desrtoy them, langoKamo will-use computers to validate each new langoKamo-word.

* Mcs.affixKmo,
* Mcs.strrUntLigKmo.affix,
